<rate>5</rate><Text>I blew up my 2003 350z engine and shopped multiple places for a replacement and installation. After a lot of shopping around and some major fails by other businesses I found SCAP on a recommendation from a friend.

I felt like I won the lottery when my install was $1,700 less than I budgeted for the closest competitive quote and it was done by SCAP ahead of schedule.

Before I found SCAP I had ordered an engine online that never showed up and the other shop held my car for a week and never even started the install after promising it would be done in 3 days.

SCAP was $1000 less than the closest installation quote, and the engine they provided was $700 cheaper than the best deal I could find online.

I am absolutely sure that those that are giving this place a 5 star review either have never stayed while their pet is groomed or don't care about their animal.  I should have followed my intuition when the lady that answered the phone sounded annoyed and inconvenienced by me calling, but I was actually excited that a place had good reviews especially for nail trimming.  I have 4 dogs that are literally my babies and treated with respect and great care.  Three of them let me trim their nails without too much fuss, but I go slow and file first, etc.  My 4th baby is nervous by nature and is impossible to cut.  I have taken him to the vet and a few choice groomers over the years and always explain his fear as well as mine of cutting too short and to please be cautious.  I'm nervous about it as his nails get long quick and have a tendency to curve towards the pads. This combined with my fear of someone hurting him lets him go to long between trims.  I searched far and wide for a new person and was excited to find Pet styling with good reviews.  To keep this review from going on forever.  My baby was handed back to me by a rude and unprofessional lady with all 10 nails bleeding. She proceeded to tell me it was my fault and treated me like an idiot.  The owner came out and was nice to talk with, but obviously allows employees to be uninformed about the safe length of a dogs nails.   No matter how long they are, you don't chop extremely short.  I have never seen a dog's nails this short.  On a different note, while I was waiting for my dog, I watched the 6 dogs being groomed.  It was so sad. She just ripped the rats out of its ears.  Everyone looked like uncaring robots..... not a place I would ever take a pet I truly cared about. The end result may look pretty, but your pet is suffering in uncaring hands in the mean time.< /Review>
